 " The film 'mad About Dance' is the story of a boy named Aarav who has a passion for dance
 aarav padhai ke bahaane shefield jaataa he vahaan ke mashhoor dancer sijar ke group main shaamil hone
 But he loses to a protégé of Caesar and then forms a group of Asian boys to confront Aarav Caesar's group
 aarav sapana dekhtaa he bharat kaa ek daancing group banaakar world dance comptishan main hissaa lene kaa
 In 'mad About Dance', there is a good sense of friendship besides dance passion
 inaki haar or jeet ke jashn hai
 There are many forms of dance in small pieces, such as locking, popping, break dance, free style dance etc
 
 
 magar dance par aadhaarit hote hue bhi film main dance kii kami he
 Dance is a passion, but dance is shown in three to four pieces of competition
 daancing ke liye acha sangeet bhi jaruri he, us lihaaj se film kaa mujeec kamjor he
 There is a struggle to win the dance competition and form a group, but the story is very slow
 junun se ek or baat yaad ai ki jis tarah film ke kirdaar aarav ko dance se lagaav he lagata he, is kirdaar ko nibhaane vaale sahil prem ko bhi dance par film banane kii kuch aisi hi khwaahish thi
 Perhaps that's why Sahil is also a writer of the film, a musician, a director and an actor
 meri najar main yah ek aisi film he jo aam darshakon kaa shaayad manoranjan na kar paae, isliye is film ke liye ke meri reating he 2 star
 
 
 a social activist filed an application in the Bombay High Court urging the CBI to direct the Union Home Minister Sushil Kumar Shinde to be an accused in the Adarsh society scam as he allegedly owns a benami flat in the building
 adarsh socity ke sadasyon par dhan shodhan kaa aarope lagane or sibiai ke saath pravartan nideshaalay kii jaanch kii maang karne vaale praveen vaategankar ne apane aavedan main scindia par aarope lagaae
 Wategaonkar claims that as Chief Minister of Maharashtra, Shinde had handled the files related to Adarsh and he allegedly owns a benami flat in this luxurious building in South Mumbai
 vaategankar kaa aarope he ki scindia ne socity ke sadsy ke rup main major en

 pradhanmantri modi ne iconomik times se kaha he ki jaldi hi autosector apane paanv par khadaa ho jayega
 The finance minister has met representatives of the auto sector
 bharat ke auto sector main is tarah kaa sankat kabhi nahin aayaa
 Major big companies are periodically shutting down their production
 iskaa asar theke par kaam karne waalon par to padataa hi hoga
 Our colleague Harbans went to Giridih in Jharkhand
 yahaan kii kai factriyon main taala lag gaya he
 Hundreds of people have become unemployed
 in logon ne twitor par apni berojgaare trend nahin karai he jaise ki in dinon har baat par trend ho jaataa he
 Production has stalled in many factories in Adityapur industrial area of jamshedpur
 april se lekar agast maheene main 700-800 factriyaan band ho gai hai
 Most of the factories produce related to Tata Motors
 tata motors main bhi block ho rahaa he
 That is, production is decreasing
 is kaaran in factriyon main utpaadan thapp hai
 Between April and August, 700 to 800 small and medium factories are closed
 motor parts se judi in factriyon main kaam nahin he
 55 factories have closed since 1 August
 iske kaaran 25000 se 3 xxrep 4 0 adhik mazaduron kaa kaam chalaa gaya he
 30,000 people lost their jobs in one place, there is no discussion anywhere
 monsoon ke samay vaise maang kam hoti he lekin is baar maang zarurat se zyada kam he is kaaran utpaadan roka ja rahaa he
 Somewhere there is a block of two days, somewhere for a week or else the factory is completely stalled
 maang main kami ke alaava kai kaaran bataae ja rahe hai
 Increase of 38 percent electricity rate from superfluous tax
 is kaaran utpaadan laagat adhik ho gai he
 Make in India is getting such a big shock, it is not even discussed in India
 sthaneey akhabaaron main taale latakane kii khabaren hai
 Contractor laborers have been affected
 unka kaam chhin gaya he
 Those who are permanent workers have got only 15 days of work
 yani aadhe din ke vetan par inhen apana ghar chalaanaa pad rahaa he
 There is also news from Pune that the auto factories there are not producing for a few days in a month
 ise industry kii bhashaa main block kehete hai
 If there is no work for four days or 15 days then you will not get salary for that day, you will not get wages
 yahi haal aapane chennai main dekha or jharkhand main bhi
 The Federation of Automobile Associations, Fada, says that more than 2
5 million people work in the auto sector
 25 lakh log or kisi na kisi rup main jude hai
 The condition of this sector involving 5 million people is bad
 bataaya ja rahaa he ki auto sector main 2 se 3 lakh logon kii naukari gai he
 Those who work on contract are not accounted for
 217 sho room desh bhar main band hue hai
 Siam is an institution in the automobile sector
 sosayadi of indian automobile manuphaccrers yani jo auto sector kii companiyaan hai unka sanghathan he siam
 SIAM says that only 24 percent of the vehicles are sold in the month of June
 iske pehle ke maheenon main bhi utpaadan or bikri main girawatt kii khabaren aa rahi thim
 Sales of two-wheelers along with cars have also come down
 uttarakhand ke chamoli jile main sthit badrinaath or hemkund sahib kii yatra sadak ke marammat ke baad shuru kar di gayi he
 The journey was suspended on Sunday due to landslides on the main road due to landslides
 badrinaath rajmarg par fanse yatriyon kii madad ke liye sena ke jawan bhi lagaaye gayi the
 Official sources said a landslide occurred in Pandukeshwar and Vishnu Prayag areas of Chamoli district on Tuesday, which led to the closure of the road and halting the journey
 chamoli jile ke jiladhikari niraj semwal ne bataaya ki seemaa sadak sanghathan or police ke kareeb 200 karmchaariyon ko malba saaf karne or sadak kii marammat karne ke liye tainaat kiya gayatha
 The work of clearing the debris was done rapidly and the road was opened for vehicles on Tuesday afternoon
 unhone bataaya ki govindghat main lungar lagaakar yatriyon ko muft main bhojan diya gaya
